(() => {
  if (
    document.cookie.split(';').some((item) => item.trim().indexOf('ckns_id=') > -1)
  ) {
    return;
  }

  try {
    var dismissCount = Number(window.localStorage.getItem('sign-in-banner-news-homepage-dismiss-count'));
    if (dismissCount >= 4) {
      return;
    }

    var lastDismissedDate = Number(window.localStorage.getItem('sign-in-banner-news-homepage-last-dismissed-date'));
    var currentTime = Date.now();
    if (currentTime - lastDismissedDate < 864000000) {
      return;
    }

    document.querySelector('html').classList.add('display-sign-in-banner');
  } catch (error) {
    return;
  }
})()

  document.addEventListener(
    'DOMContentLoaded',
    () => {
      const validNations = ['uk', 'england', 'scotland', 'wales', 'northern_ireland'];
      
      const nation = window.localStorage.getItem('nation_preference');
      
      if (validNations.includes(nation) && nation !== 'uk') {
        const containerToDisplay = document.querySelector("#nations-news-" + nation);
        const containerToHide = document.querySelector("#nations-news-uk");
  
        if (containerToDisplay) {
          if (containerToHide) {
            containerToHide.setAttribute('hidden', '');
          }

          containerToDisplay.removeAttribute('hidden');
        }
      }
    },
    { once: true }
  );
